-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+# Nunchucks&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- Go runtime + CLI&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- WASM target from Go&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- Playground editor demo with live preview&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+## Current Focus&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+## Installation&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+```bash&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+```&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+```ts&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &amp;quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&amp;quot;;&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+  wasmURL: &amp;quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&amp;quot;,&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+  goURL: &amp;quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&amp;quot;,&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+});&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+const html = nc.renderFromMap({&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+  template: &amp;quot;index.njk&amp;quot;,&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+  files: { &amp;quot;index.njk&amp;quot;: &amp;quot;Hello {{ name }}&amp;quot; },&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+  context: { name: &amp;quot;world&amp;quot; },&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+});&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+```&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+### CLI&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+macOS and Linux:&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+nunchucks version&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+nunchucks help&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+```powershell&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+# Nunchucks&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- Go runtime + CLI&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- WASM target from Go&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+- Playground editor demo with live preview&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+## Current Focus&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+&lt;/span&gt;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-&lt;span class=&quot;diffline add&quot;&gt;+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.&lt;/span&gt;</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+# Nunchucks</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Go runtime + CLI</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- WASM target from Go</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Playground editor demo with live preview</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Current Focus</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Installation</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```ts</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&quot;;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  wasmURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  goURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+});</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+const html = nc.renderFromMap({</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  template: &quot;index.njk&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  files: { &quot;index.njk&quot;: &quot;Hello {{ name }}&quot; },</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  context: { name: &quot;world&quot; },</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+});</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### CLI</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+macOS and Linux:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks version</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks help</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Windows PowerShell:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```powershell</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks.exe version</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks.exe help</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Go users can also install from source:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### Go usage</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+cd go</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go test ./...</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Go CLI</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -views ./views \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -template index.njk \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -views ./views \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -out ./public \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Go Examples</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./examples/basic</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./examples/advanced</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./examples/client</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## WASM Build (Go)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+GOOS=js GOARCH=wasm go build -o wasm/nunchucks.wasm ./cmd/nunchucks-wasm</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+cp &quot;$(go env GOROOT)/lib/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot; wasm/wasm_exec.js</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Stateless Playground Render Server (Go)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+A stateless memory-render API is available under `go/server`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./server</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Default endpoint:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `POST /api/playground/render`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `GET /healthz`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+See `go/server/README.md` for request/response format.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Docs</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Docs source is in `docs/` and is intended for GitHub Pages.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Architecture docs:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `SSR.md` (server-side rendering behavior)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `CLIENT_RENDERING.md` (client-side behavior and roadmap)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Key pages:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `docs/index.html` (main docs)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `docs/templating.html` (templating reference)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `docs/playground.html` (mini editor + preview)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Local App Builder (Live Reload + Playground)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+A local builder is available in `app/` to edit template files, add files, and preview output in one page with file watching.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Run:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+pnpm app</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Open:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `http://localhost:5177`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Notes:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `app/views` is the file workspace.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Rendering uses the Go playground server API (started automatically by `app/server.mjs`).</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Tests</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### Go</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```ts</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&quot;;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  wasmURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  goURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+});</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+const html = nc.renderFromMap({</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  template: &quot;index.njk&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  files: { &quot;index.njk&quot;: &quot;Hello {{ name }}&quot; },</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  context: { name: &quot;world&quot; },</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+});</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### CLI</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+macOS and Linux:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks version</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks help</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Windows PowerShell:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```powershell</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks.exe version</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+nunchucks.exe help</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Go users can also install from source:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### Go usage</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+cd go</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go test ./...</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Go CLI</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -views ./views \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -template index.njk \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -views ./views \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -out ./public \</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Go Examples</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./examples/basic</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./examples/advanced</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./examples/client</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## WASM Build (Go)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+GOOS=js GOARCH=wasm go build -o wasm/nunchucks.wasm ./cmd/nunchucks-wasm</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+cp &quot;$(go env GOROOT)/lib/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot; wasm/wasm_exec.js</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Stateless Playground Render Server (Go)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+A stateless memory-render API is available under `go/server`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+go run ./server</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Default endpoint:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `POST /api/playground/render`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `GET /healthz`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+See `go/server/README.md` for request/response format.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Docs</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Docs source is in `docs/` and is intended for GitHub Pages.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Architecture docs:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `SSR.md` (server-side rendering behavior)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `CLIENT_RENDERING.md` (client-side behavior and roadmap)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Key pages:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `docs/index.html` (main docs)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `docs/templating.html` (templating reference)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `docs/playground.html` (mini editor + preview)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Local App Builder (Live Reload + Playground)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+A local builder is available in `app/` to edit template files, add files, and preview output in one page with file watching.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Run:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+pnpm app</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Open:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `http://localhost:5177`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Notes:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `app/views` is the file workspace.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Rendering uses the Go playground server API (started automatically by `app/server.mjs`).</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Tests</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+# Nunchucks</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Go runtime + CLI</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- WASM target from Go</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Playground editor demo with live preview</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Current Focus</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+## Installation</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```bash</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```ts</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&quot;;</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  wasmURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  goURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+});</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+const html = nc.renderFromMap({</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  template: &quot;index.njk&quot;,</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  files: { &quot;index.njk&quot;: &quot;Hello {{ name }}&quot; },</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+  context: { name: &quot;world&quot; },</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+});</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+### CLI</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+From `go/`:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+```</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+Default endpoint:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>

-<span class="diffline del">-+Notes:</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- `app/views` is the file workspace.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.</span>
-<span class="diffline del">-+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.</span>

--<span class="diffline add">+# Nunchucks</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Go runtime + CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- WASM target from Go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Playground editor demo with live preview</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Current Focus</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Installation</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```ts</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&quot;;</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  wasmURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  goURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+});</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+const html = nc.renderFromMap({</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  template: &quot;index.njk&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  files: { &quot;index.njk&quot;: &quot;Hello {{ name }}&quot; },</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  context: { name: &quot;world&quot; },</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+});</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+macOS and Linux:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Windows PowerShell:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```powershell</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks.exe version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks.exe help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Go users can also install from source:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### Go usage</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cd go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go test ./...</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Go CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -views ./views \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -template index.njk \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -views ./views \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -out ./public \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Go Examples</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/basic</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/advanced</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/client</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## WASM Build (Go)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+GOOS=js GOARCH=wasm go build -o wasm/nunchucks.wasm ./cmd/nunchucks-wasm</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cp &quot;$(go env GOROOT)/lib/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot; wasm/wasm_exec.js</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Stateless Playground Render Server (Go)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+A stateless memory-render API is available under `go/server`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./server</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Default endpoint:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `POST /api/playground/render`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `GET /healthz`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+See `go/server/README.md` for request/response format.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Docs</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Docs source is in `docs/` and is intended for GitHub Pages.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Architecture docs:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `SSR.md` (server-side rendering behavior)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `CLIENT_RENDERING.md` (client-side behavior and roadmap)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Key pages:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/index.html` (main docs)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/templating.html` (templating reference)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/playground.html` (mini editor + preview)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Local App Builder (Live Reload + Playground)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+A local builder is available in `app/` to edit template files, add files, and preview output in one page with file watching.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Run:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+pnpm app</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Open:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `http://localhost:5177`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Notes:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `app/views` is the file workspace.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Rendering uses the Go playground server API (started automatically by `app/server.mjs`).</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Tests</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### Go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cd go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go test ./...</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Status</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+This repo is under active development. Some advanced parity edge cases and async behavior are still being iterated.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>

--<span class="diffline add">+# Nunchucks</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Go runtime + CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- WASM target from Go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Playground editor demo with live preview</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Current Focus</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Installation</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```ts</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&quot;;</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  wasmURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  goURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+});</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+const html = nc.renderFromMap({</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  template: &quot;index.njk&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  files: { &quot;index.njk&quot;: &quot;Hello {{ name }}&quot; },</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  context: { name: &quot;world&quot; },</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+});</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+macOS and Linux:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Windows PowerShell:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```powershell</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks.exe version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks.exe help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Go users can also install from source:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### Go usage</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cd go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go test ./...</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Go CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -views ./views \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -template index.njk \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -views ./views \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -out ./public \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Go Examples</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/basic</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/advanced</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/client</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## WASM Build (Go)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+GOOS=js GOARCH=wasm go build -o wasm/nunchucks.wasm ./cmd/nunchucks-wasm</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cp &quot;$(go env GOROOT)/lib/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot; wasm/wasm_exec.js</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Stateless Playground Render Server (Go)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+A stateless memory-render API is available under `go/server`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./server</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Default endpoint:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `POST /api/playground/render`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `GET /healthz`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+See `go/server/README.md` for request/response format.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Docs</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Docs source is in `docs/` and is intended for GitHub Pages.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Architecture docs:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `SSR.md` (server-side rendering behavior)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `CLIENT_RENDERING.md` (client-side behavior and roadmap)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Key pages:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/index.html` (main docs)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/templating.html` (templating reference)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/playground.html` (mini editor + preview)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Local App Builder (Live Reload + Playground)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+A local builder is available in `app/` to edit template files, add files, and preview output in one page with file watching.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Run:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+pnpm app</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Open:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `http://localhost:5177`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Notes:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `app/views` is the file workspace.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Rendering uses the Go playground server API (started automatically by `app/server.mjs`).</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Tests</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### Go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cd go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go test ./...</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Status</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+This repo is under active development. Some advanced parity edge cases and async behavior are still being iterated.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>

--<span class="diffline add">+# Nunchucks</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Go runtime + CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- WASM target from Go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Playground editor demo with live preview</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Current Focus</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Installation</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```ts</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from &quot;@samuelbines/nunchucks&quot;;</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  wasmURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  goURL: &quot;/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+});</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+const html = nc.renderFromMap({</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  template: &quot;index.njk&quot;,</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  files: { &quot;index.njk&quot;: &quot;Hello {{ name }}&quot; },</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  context: { name: &quot;world&quot; },</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+});</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+macOS and Linux:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Windows PowerShell:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```powershell</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks.exe version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+nunchucks.exe help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Go users can also install from source:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### Go usage</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cd go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go test ./...</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Go CLI</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -views ./views \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -template index.njk \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -views ./views \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -out ./public \</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+  -data '{&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Hello&quot;}'</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Go Examples</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/basic</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/advanced</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./examples/client</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## WASM Build (Go)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+GOOS=js GOARCH=wasm go build -o wasm/nunchucks.wasm ./cmd/nunchucks-wasm</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cp &quot;$(go env GOROOT)/lib/wasm/wasm_exec.js&quot; wasm/wasm_exec.js</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Stateless Playground Render Server (Go)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+A stateless memory-render API is available under `go/server`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+From `go/`:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go run ./server</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Default endpoint:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `POST /api/playground/render`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `GET /healthz`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+See `go/server/README.md` for request/response format.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Docs</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Docs source is in `docs/` and is intended for GitHub Pages.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Architecture docs:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `SSR.md` (server-side rendering behavior)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `CLIENT_RENDERING.md` (client-side behavior and roadmap)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Key pages:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/index.html` (main docs)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/templating.html` (templating reference)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `docs/playground.html` (mini editor + preview)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Local App Builder (Live Reload + Playground)</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+A local builder is available in `app/` to edit template files, add files, and preview output in one page with file watching.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Run:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+pnpm app</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Open:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `http://localhost:5177`</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+Notes:</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- `app/views` is the file workspace.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+- Rendering uses the Go playground server API (started automatically by `app/server.mjs`).</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Tests</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+### Go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```bash</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+cd go</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+go test ./...</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+```</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+## Status</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+This repo is under active development. Some advanced parity edge cases and async behavior are still being iterated.</span>
--<span class="diffline add">+</span>

--+# Nunchucks
--+
--+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:
--+
--+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)
--+- Go runtime + CLI
--+- WASM target from Go
--+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)
--+- Playground editor demo with live preview
--+
--+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`
--+
--+## Current Focus
--+
--+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.
--+
--+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.
--+
--+## Installation
--+
--+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)
--+
--+```bash
--+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks
--+```
--+
--+```ts
--+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from "@samuelbines/nunchucks";
--+
--+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({
--+  wasmURL: "/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm",
--+  goURL: "/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js",
--+});
--+
--+const html = nc.renderFromMap({
--+  template: "index.njk",
--+  files: { "index.njk": "Hello {{ name }}" },
--+  context: { name: "world" },
--+});
--+```
--+
--+### CLI
--+
--+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:
--+
--+macOS and Linux:
--+
--+```bash
--+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh
--+nunchucks version
--+nunchucks help
--+```
--+
--+Windows PowerShell:
--+
--+```powershell
--+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex
--+nunchucks.exe version
--+nunchucks.exe help
--+```
--+
--+Go users can also install from source:
--+
--+```bash
--+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest
--+```
--+
--+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.
--+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.
--+
--+### Go usage
--+
--+```bash
--+cd go
--+go test ./...
--+```
--+
--+## Go CLI
--+
--+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:
--+
--+```bash
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version
--+
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \
--+  -views ./views \
--+  -template index.njk \
--+  -data '{"title":"Hello"}'
--+
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \
--+  -views ./views \
--+  -out ./public \
--+  -data '{"title":"Hello"}'
--+```
--+
--+## Go Examples
--+
--+From `go/`:
--+
--+```bash
--+go run ./examples/basic
--+go run ./examples/advanced
--+go run ./examples/client
--+```
--+
--+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.
--+
--+## WASM Build (Go)
--+
--+From `go/`:
--+
--+```bash
--+GOOS=js GOARCH=wasm go build -o wasm/nunchucks.wasm ./cmd/nunchucks-wasm
--+cp "$(go env GOROOT)/lib/wasm/wasm_exec.js" wasm/wasm_exec.js
--+```
--+
--+## Stateless Playground Render Server (Go)
--+
--+A stateless memory-render API is available under `go/server`.
--+
--+From `go/`:
--+
--+```bash
--+go run ./server
--+```
--+
--+Default endpoint:
--+
--+- `POST /api/playground/render`
--+- `GET /healthz`
--+
--+See `go/server/README.md` for request/response format.
--+
--+## Docs
--+
--+Docs source is in `docs/` and is intended for GitHub Pages.
--+
--+Architecture docs:
--+
--+- `SSR.md` (server-side rendering behavior)
--+- `CLIENT_RENDERING.md` (client-side behavior and roadmap)
--+
--+Key pages:
--+
--+- `docs/index.html` (main docs)
--+- `docs/templating.html` (templating reference)
--+- `docs/playground.html` (mini editor + preview)
--+
--+## Local App Builder (Live Reload + Playground)
--+
--+A local builder is available in `app/` to edit template files, add files, and preview output in one page with file watching.
--+
--+Run:
--+
--+```bash
--+pnpm app
--+```
--+
--+Open:
--+
--+- `http://localhost:5177`
--+
--+Notes:
--+
--+- `app/views` is the file workspace.
--+- Saving from the UI writes to `app/views`.
--+- File changes in `app/views` trigger live refresh.
--+- Rendering uses the Go playground server API (started automatically by `app/server.mjs`).
--+
--+## Tests
--+
--+### Go
--+
--+```bash
--+cd go
--+go test ./...
--+```
--+
--+## Status
--+
--+This repo is under active development. Some advanced parity edge cases and async behavior are still being iterated.

--+Open an issue or PR on GitHub.

--+# Nunchucks
--+
--+Nunchucks is a templating project with Nunchucks-first syntax and Jinja-style concepts:
--+
--+- JavaScript/TypeScript package backed by Go WASM (`@samuelbines/nunchucks`)
--+- Go runtime + CLI
--+- WASM target from Go
--+- Docs site in `docs/` (GitHub Pages)
--+- Playground editor demo with live preview
--+
--+Repository: `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks`
--+
--+## Current Focus
--+
--+This project is actively evolving toward strong syntax parity plus a multi-language workflow.
--+
--+Implemented in Go today includes core tags (`if`, `for`, `set`, `extends`, `block`, `include`, `macro`, `import`, `call`, `raw`, `verbatim`, `filter`), expression engine improvements, and a broad set of built-in filters.
--+
--+## Installation
--+
--+### JS/TS package (Go WASM runtime)
--+
--+```bash
--+npm install @samuelbines/nunchucks
--+```
--+
--+```ts
--+import { loadNunchucksWasm } from "@samuelbines/nunchucks";
--+
--+const nc = await loadNunchucksWasm({
--+  wasmURL: "/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/nunchucks.wasm",
--+  goURL: "/node_modules/@samuelbines/nunchucks/go/wasm/wasm_exec.js",
--+});
--+
--+const html = nc.renderFromMap({
--+  template: "index.njk",
--+  files: { "index.njk": "Hello {{ name }}" },
--+  context: { name: "world" },
--+});
--+```
--+
--+### CLI
--+
--+Install the native CLI from GitHub Releases:
--+
--+macOS and Linux:
--+
--+```bash
--+curl -fsSL https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.sh | sh
--+nunchucks version
--+nunchucks help
--+```
--+
--+Windows PowerShell:
--+
--+```powershell
--+irm https://raw.githubusercontent.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/main/scripts/install-cli.ps1 | iex
--+nunchucks.exe version
--+nunchucks.exe help
--+```
--+
--+Go users can also install from source:
--+
--+```bash
--+go install github.com/SamuelDBines/nunjucks/go/cmd/nunchucks@latest
--+```
--+
--+Release binaries are published at `https://github.com/SamuelDBines/nunchucks/releases`.
--+The install scripts pick a writable bin directory and print PATH instructions when needed.
--+
--+### Go usage
--+
--+```bash
--+cd go
--+go test ./...
--+```
--+
--+## Go CLI
--+
--+From `go/` or from an installed release binary:
--+
--+```bash
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks help render
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks version
--+
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks render \
--+  -views ./views \
--+  -template index.njk \
--+  -data '{"title":"Hello"}'
--+
--+go run ./cmd/nunchucks precompile \
--+  -views ./views \
--+  -out ./public \
--+  -data '{"title":"Hello"}'
--+```
--+
--+## Go Examples
--+
--+From `go/`:
--+
--+```bash
--+go run ./examples/basic
--+go run ./examples/advanced
--+go run ./examples/client
--+```
--+
--+Also see sample templates under `samples/go`.

--+From `go/`:
